This macro enables automatic generation of type-safe Rust APIs for both client-side (procedural macros) and server-side (compiler) implementations.\\n\\nThe bridge defines server API operations including:\\n- TokenStream manipulation (create, clone, to_string, from_str)\\n- Span operations (debug, parent, source, byte_range, etc.)\\n- Symbol normalization and validation\\n- Literal creation and manipulation\\n- Diagnostic emission\\n\\n**library/proc_macro/src/bridge/client.rs**: Implements client-side handle types and encoding/decoding logic for the bridge protocol.\\n\\n**library/proc_macro/src/bridge/server.rs**: Implements server-side implementations of the bridge API traits.\\n\\n#### Compiler-Side Integration\\n\\n**compiler/rustc_expand/src/proc_macro_server.rs**: The compiler's implementation of the proc_macro bridge server.
